Nope
For contributing, u need to first select one project then learn by urself on that topic, see the issues in GitHub issue section, select one, say pls assign this issue to me, they will assign it to you, tell them how you will contribute to the issue, if they like how u will contribute they will say ok, if not then make changes accordingly. After finallising on what u need to do. Fork the repo to ur GitHub profile. Clone the repo to ur local pc, initialize git, set upstream to the forked repo in ur profile, make a branch based on the topic u will be working on ( this branch has name called feature branch ) after u made the necessary changes to the project that the supervisor asked u to make, push the repo to ur local repo in GitHub profile by typing git push in command line. Then make a pulk request from ur local repo in GitHub profile to the orginal repo u forked from. Supervisor will review ur changes if they like what u did, they will merge it with the original repo, if they don't like it, they will say to make the necessary changes again, make the changes ask them again if it's ok, loop will continue until u either give up or they merge ur pull request

Esey hei mera approach bata raha mene code karke test nahi kiya, tum khud try kar sakte ho, I think at first u can find all the possible pairs of hideouts n check which such combination has maximum distance between them. Like { (,) & (,) } or { (,) & (,) } etc. there will be HC combination. Since constraints is only <= I think u can have a time complexity of O(n^) so try to find such a approach which fits this time constraint usually time constraints are also a hint to the approah u can take.
Since all the cities are connected to each other so all hideouts will also be connected to each other so all possible pairs will be valid so no need to check if pairs r valid u can just check which pair combination will have max distance

DOS Attack: DOS means Denial of Services, is an attack where the legitimate or authorized user of the system does not get access to the system because some other illegitimate or unauthorized user unnecessarily making the system busy. Often this type of attacks is done by some other application. Where the application continuously starts submitting a request and creates a pool of requests and the server gets totally engaged in replying the. And you suffer from starvation.

An AVL tree T is a binary search tree in which every internal node v of T are height balanced, i.e. the heights of the children of v differ by at most . In this assignment, you are to perform various operations on an AVL tree. You may choose the type of data in a node of your choice. You may additionally add a field for maintaining the difference in height of the subtrees in the node structure.
